< review>
Can't say enough great things about Dave and the entire crew at Grizzly. We started working with them about two years ago (when our winery moved into a new location) and the experience could not have been better. Dave came out for an estimate, we talked through a few different options and he put together a super-competitive quote (one that even included some of my thoughts). When it came time for install...Dave and John were there on time and even managed to finish the job ahead of schedule. It is worth noting that we had several different trades in the building at the same time...but that didn't seem to bother them at all. After things were wrapped up, Dave took the time to program each component of the system and go over all the specifics (it's kind of a complicated set-up...at least for a novice like me).

And their service after the fact is spot on as well. We've had to call them out a couple of times for issues (equipment defects) and they have always come through...usually within an hour or two. For our money...Dave and the folks at Grizzly are just the best.<//review>

< review>
Always stocked with a great selection and they always have good deals and friendly employees. Since Covid though, they have been mistakenly charging me sales tax on all of my purchases, despite me using a medical card (which should exempt me). This has added up to a lot of money over time. Also their rewards system always applies backwards if your buying an item on sale. For example, I twice bought an item that was on sale for 25% off that was $25 and I used my $10 off reward. Rather than discounting the item 25% off and then applying the rewards at the end of the purchase (as most stores would) they do it the other way around. This results in a difference of $2.50. This is not a huge difference, but stores should be aware if they are unfairly overcharging customers regularly. I have shopped here a ton and will continue to do so because of their great customer service, I simply hope these issues are fixed as they have cost me a decent amount of money as they have compounded over the last few months.</review>

< Text>
This is the most disorganized dispensary. There are few parking meters (1 space on back always taken). It takes a few trips around the block to park. About 15 minutes per trip. If you need change, Higher Path has none. I don‚Äôt see what‚Äôs so hard about keeping a roll of quarters around.

Next is the wait time. You wait in lobby THEN wait inside. There‚Äôs always more customers than salespeople, and it is hard to see the products. Brands of edibles vary, so it‚Äôs whatever is delivered recently is for sale. There‚Äôs also no sugar free edibles for some reason.

4/20 was a bust. A long line for a tour, no freebies, only things on sale were very expensive and the website contained little info about what was available when you get to the store.

I‚Äôd call first to talk to a salesperson. Order with them on their website (while you have them on the phone), so you can confirm the website items are actually in the store. If you‚Äôre driving, you‚Äôll need extra time to find parking. I suggest a bus or an Uber.</Text>

<Resp>{'time': 1555699894980, 'text': "Hey Kel! We actually don't get to decide what taxes we charge--that is dictated by the city of Los Angeles and the state of California. As a legal, licensed dispensary we are required by law to charge these taxes otherwise we could lose our license. To break it down for you, recreational consumers (individuals without a medical recommendation) pay the most in taxes--10% Local Tax and 9.5% Sales Tax which you can see on your receipt. There's also a 15% State Excise Tax that is included in the prices of our products, so you won't see that one separately on your receipt. Patients with a medical recommendation from a doctor pay 5% Local Tax and 9.5% Sales Tax, as well as that 15% State Excise Tax included in the product price. Individuals with an MMIC from the county save the most on taxes--they pay 5% Local Tax and the 15% State Excise Tax included in the product price. We completely understand your frustration about the taxes and the desire to save as much as possible, which is why we do offer deals like our $60 Half Oz Specials, $25 budlet 1/8ths, a variety of 1/8ths at $30-$40 and Dollar Joint Fridays as well as other special text deals and Vendor Day deals. Any dispensary that you visit that isn't charging you these taxes isn't legal and we'd caution you against shopping at illegal dispensaries since the products on their shelves don't have to be regulated or tested for your safety in any way. If you have any questions about our prices or taxes, please feel free to email us at info@thehigherpath.com and we'll be happy to assist you :) -The Higher Path Staff"}< /Resp><Rating>2< /Rating>< Pics>

{'time': 1549655465627, 'text': 'Hey Ismael--sorry to hear you didn\'t enjoy your visit with us. The reason you can\'t "smell what you\'re buying" is per Bureau of Cannabis Control regulations--cannabis products sold at licensed dispensaries in California must leave the store in sealed packages, meaning that we legally cannot open the package you\'re buying for you to smell it. We do change out the sample jars every time we get a fresh batch of a strain in (sometimes more frequently if the bud in the jar seems to have lost its smell), so the flower you\'re looking at/smelling IS from the same harvest as what you\'re purchasing--definitely not "false advertising" as you stated in your review. The new packaging that flower is required to be in keeps it fresh on the shelf for longer--the containers are sealed after the fresh flower is packaged & they will not lose freshness until after the package has been opened by the consumer. One of our brands High Pack actually uses liquid nitrogen to keep sealed flower fresh on the shelf for up to 2 years. The cannabis industry is changing--gone are the days of buds being stored in large glass jars & weighed out for you when you purchase them. This is to ensure that every product is clean, tested and safe for the consumer. Any shop you go to that isn\'t selling you prepackaged flower isn\'t legal--you can check out the BCC website to read more about California laws & regulations for legal cannabis https://www.bcc.ca.gov/law_regs/index.html. The amount of time that passes between a strain being harvested & packaged has to do with the fact that it has to undergo testing & pass all Phase III requirements before it can be packaged & sold to a dispensary, so it\'s totally normal to see a harvest date that is months before a packaged date. Back when flower didn\'t need to be tested before being sold, there was significantly less time in between something being harvested & put on the shelf for sale. If you have further questions about our products or the new laws & regulations please feel free to email us at info@thehigherpath.com & we\'ll be happy to assist you :) -The Higher Path Staff'}</Response>
